SESSION HOOKS: Analytics Entry/Exit Points\n\n### 2.1 session-start Hook\n**When:** Every new Claude Code session  \n**Location:** `.claude/hooks/session-start.js`  \n**Analytics Invoked:**\n\n```\n1. Dependency hash check (package-lock.json, functions/package-lock.json)\n2. Pattern compliance check: node scripts/check-pattern-compliance.js\n3. Auto-consolidation: node scripts/run-consolidation.js --auto\n4. Review sync: npm run reviews:sync --apply\n5. Commit log sync: node scripts/seed-commit-log.js --sync\n6. Archive rotation: reviews.jsonl (>50 entries), hook-warnings-log.jsonl (>50), health-score-log.jsonl (>30)\n7. TDMS health check: reads metrics.json, warns on S0 count, S1 threshold\n8. Health quick check: node scripts/health/run-health-check.js --quick\n```\n\n**State Files Modified:**\n- `.claude/.lockfile-hash` (package-lock.json hash)\n- `.claude/.functions-lockfile-hash` (functions/package-lock.json hash)\n- `.claude/hooks/.session-state.json` (session begin/end tracking)\n- `.claude/state/reviews.jsonl` (synced from markdown)\n- `.claude/state/hook-warnings-log.jsonl` (rotated if >50 entries)\n- `.claude/state/health-score-log.jsonl` (rotated if >30 entries)\n\n**Output Surfaces:**\n- Console: Installation status, pattern violations, consolidation status, TDMS S0/S1 counts, health score\n- Exit Code: 0 = success with warnings, warnings logged as counts\n\n**Scope:** NON-BLOCKING (all failures continue with warnings)\n\n---\n\n### 2.2 session-end Hook (Manual via `/session-end` command)\n**When:** User runs `/session-end` skill or `npm run session:end`  \n**Location:** `scripts/session-end-commit.js`  \n**Analytics Invoked:**\n\n```\n1. Git status & changed files count\n2. Debt state validation: reads MASTER_DEBT.jsonl\n3. Learning effectiveness: recent improvements & patterns promoted\n4. Velocity log: entries since session start\n5. Session log: session notes (from SESSION_CONTEXT.md)\n6. Arc completion check: completion percentage\n7. Phase completion check: active phases\n8. Hook analytics: override frequencies, failure counts\n```\n\n**State Files Modified:**\n- `.claude/state/velocity-log.jsonl` (appends session velocity)\n- `.claude/state/session-notes.json` (updates session summary)\n- `docs/ROADMAP.md` (marks completed items)\n- Git commit with session summary\n\n**Output Surfaces:**\n- Console: Session summary, velocity, learning effectiveness, debt status\n- Git commit message: Detailed session recap\n\n**Scope:** INTERACTIVE (asks user for decisions on debt, learning, artifacts)\n\n---\n\n## 3. PRE-COMMIT HOOK: Automated Enforcement Gates\n\n**Location:** `.husky/pre-commit` (1,400+ lines)  \n**Trigger:** Every `git commit`  \n**Analytics Invoked:**\n\n| Check # | Script | Blocking? | Override Var | Output |\n|---------|--------|-----------|--------------|--------|\n| 1 | `npm run lint` (ESLint) | YES (exit 1) | SKIP_CHECKS=eslint | Exit code + violations |\n| 2 | `npm test` | Conditional (doc-only skipped) | SKIP_CHECKS=tests | Exit code + failures |\n| 3 | `npx lint-staged` | YES (exit 1) | N/A | Auto-formats, exit code |\n| 4 | `node scripts/check-pattern-compliance.js --staged` | YES (exit 1) | SKIP_CHECKS=patterns | Exit code + violations (append to hook-warnings on 2) |\n| 5 | `node scripts/validate-audit.js --strict-s0s1` | YES (exit 1 if S0/S1 invalid) | SKIP_CHECKS=audit | Exit code + violations |\n| 6 | `npm run validate:canon` | WARNING (non-blocking) | N/A | Appends to hook-warnings.json if fails |\n| 7 | `npm run skills:validate` | WARNING (non-blocking) | N/A | Appends to hook-warnings.json if fails |\n| 8 | `node scripts/check-cross-doc-deps.js --trivial` | YES (exit 1) | SKIP_CHECKS=cross-doc | Exit code + violations |\n| 9 | `npm run docs:index` | AUTO-FIX (non-blocking) | SKIP_CHECKS=doc-index | Auto-stages DOCUMENTATION_INDEX.md |\n| 10 | `node scripts/check-doc-headers.js` | YES for new docs (exit 1) | SKIP_CHECKS=doc-header | Exit code + violations |\n| 11 | `node scripts/check-agent-compliance.js` | WARNING (non-blocking) | STRICT_AGENT_CHECK | Appends to hook-warnings.json if --strict fails |\n| 12 | `node scripts/debt/validate-schema.js --staged-only` | YES (exit 1) | SKIP_CHECKS=debt | Exit code + schema violations |\n\n**State Files Modified:**\n- `.claude/override-log.jsonl` (logged via `node scripts/log-override.js` when SKIP_CHECKS used)\n- `.claude/state/hook-warnings-log.jsonl` (appended for non-blocking warnings)\n- `.git/hook-output.log` (all hook output for debugging)\n\n**Output Surfaces:**\n- Console: Pass/fail per check, skip reasons, violations\n- Exit Code: 1 = commit blocked, 0 = commit allowed\n- Log File: `.git/hook-output.log` persists all output\n\n**Override Mechanism:**\n```bash\nSKIP_CHECKS=\"patterns,cross-doc\" SKIP_REASON=\"reason (10-500 chars)\" git commit\n```\nAll overrides logged to `.claude/override-log.jsonl` for audit trail.\n\n---\n\n## 4. PRE-PUSH HOOK: Secondary Gate\n\n**Location:** `.husky/pre-push` (140+ lines)  \n**Trigger:** Every `git push` (to any branch)  \n**Analytics Invoked:**\n\n| Check | Script | Blocking? | Output |\n|-------|--------|-----------|--------|\n| 1 | `npm run deps:circular` | YES (exit 1) | Exit code + cycle paths |\n| 2 | `node scripts/check-pattern-compliance.js` (push diff only) | WARNING (non-blocking) | Appends to hook-warnings.json |\n| 3 | `check code-reviewer invocation` for script changes | WARNING (non-blocking) | Appends to hook-warnings.json |\n\n**State Files Modified:**\n- `.claude/state/hook-warnings-log.jsonl` (appended if script checks fail)\n- `.claude/state/agent-invocations.jsonl` (checked for code-reviewer presence)\n\n**Output Surfaces:**\n- Console: Pass/fail per check, warnings\n- Exit Code: 1 = push blocked, 0 = push allowed\n\n---\n\n## 5. CI/CD WORKFLOWS: Automated Checks on Push/PR\n\n### 5.1 Continuous Integration (`ci.yml`)\n**Trigger:** Push to main, PR to main  \n**Checks:**\n\n| Check | Script | Blocking? | Output |\n|-------|--------|-----------|--------|\n| ESLint | `npm run lint` | YES | Exit code + violations |\n| Prettier | `npm run format:check` | YES | Exit code + diffs |\n| Circular Deps | `npm run deps:circular` | YES | Exit code + cycles |\n| Unused Deps | `npm run deps:unused` | YES (2026-02-02) | Exit code + unused list |\n| Pattern Compliance (PR) | `node scripts/check-pattern-compliance.js -- $changed_files` | YES | Exit code + violations |\n| Pattern Compliance (Push) | `npm run patterns:check-all` | WARNING (continue-on-error) | Exit code + violations |\n| Pattern Tests | `npx vitest run tests/pattern-compliance.test.js` | YES | vitest output |\n| Docs Check | `npm run docs:check` | WARNING (continue-on-error) | Exit code + issues |\n| CANON Schema | `npm run validate:canon` | YES | Exit code + violations |\n| Audit Validation | `npm run audit:validate -- --all` | WARNING (continue-on-error) | Exit code + violations |\n| TDMS Schema | `node scripts/debt/validate-schema.js` | YES (if MASTER_DEBT.jsonl exists) | Exit code + violations |\n| ROADMAP Refs | `node scripts/debt/sync-roadmap-refs.js --check-only` | YES (if MASTER_DEBT.jsonl exists) | Exit code + orphaned refs |\n| TDMS Views | `node scripts/debt/generate-views.js` + git diff | WARNING (continue-on-error) | Exit code + stale views |\n| Type Check | `npx tsc --noEmit` | YES | tsc output |\n| Tests + Coverage | `npm run test:coverage` | YES | test output + HTML coverage |\n\n**Coverage Report:** Uploaded to artifacts (14-day retention)\n\n### 5.2 Review Check Workflow (`review-check.yml`)\n**Trigger:** PR opened/updated on main  \n**Script:** `node scripts/check-review-needed.js --json`  \n**Output:**\n- Exit code: 0 = no review needed, 1 = review recommended, 2 = error\n- PR Comment: Lists triggered review thresholds\n- PR Label: Adds `needs-review` if triggered\n- Console: JSON output with triggers, recommendation\n\n### 5.3 Pattern Compliance Audit (`pattern-compliance-audit.yml`)\n**Trigger:** Weekly Monday 6am UTC or manual dispatch  \n**Script:** `node scripts/check-pattern-compliance.js --all --json`  \n**Output:**\n- Console: Blocking count, warning count, GitHub step summary\n- Artifacts: `compliance-report.json` (30-day retention)\n- GitHub Issue: Created if blocking > 0 or warnings > 75 (auto-updated weekly)\n- Labels: `pattern-compliance`, `tech-debt`\n\n### 5.4 SonarCloud Analysis (`sonarcloud.yml`)\n**Trigger:** Push to main, PR to main, manual dispatch  \n**Tool:** `SonarSource/sonarcloud-github-action`  \n**Output:**\n- SonarCloud dashboard: Code quality, security, coverage metrics\n- PR Decoration: Comments on PR with findings\n- GitHub Code Scanning: Results published (if enabled)\n\n---\n\n## 6. HEALTH CHECK SYSTEM: Continuous Monitoring\n\n**Runner:** `scripts/health/run-health-check.js`  \n**When Invoked:**\n- session-start (--quick mode, 4 fast checkers)\n- Manual: `npm run` (not a direct npm script, but invoked by skills)\n- `/alerts` skill (limited or --full mode)\n\n**Checkers (10 total):**\n| Checker | Quick? | Metrics | Output |\n|---------|--------|---------|--------|\n| Code Quality | YES | TS errors, ESLint warnings | Dimension score |\n| Security | YES | Critical/high vulns, supply chain | Dimension score |\n| Debt Health | YES | S0/S1 counts, resolution rate | Dimension score |\n| Test Coverage | YES | Pass rate, staleness | Dimension score |\n| Learning Effectiveness | NO | Effectiveness %, automation coverage | Dimension score |\n| Hook Pipeline | NO | Warning logs, override rates, false positives | Dimension score |\n| Session Management | NO | Gap hours, session duration, completeness | Dimension score |\n| Documentation | NO | Staleness, accuracy, placement | Dimension score |\n| Pattern Enforcement | NO | Violations, false positive rate | Dimension score |\n| Ecosystem Integration | NO | Audit coverage, skill compliance | Dimension score |\n\n**Composite Scoring:**\n- Start at 100, deduct 30 per error, 10 per warning\n- Grade: A(90+), B(80+), C(70+), D(60+), F(<60)\n\n**State Files Modified:**\n- `.claude/state/health-score-log.jsonl` (appends composite score)\n\n---\n\n## 7. ALERTS SKILL: Interactive Health Dashboard\n\n**Invocation:** `/alerts` or `/alerts --full`  \n**Script:** `node .claude/skills/alerts/scripts/run-alerts.js --limited` or `--full`\n\n**Limited Mode (16 categories):**\n1. Code Health (TS errors, ESLint)\n2. Security (vulns, supply chain)\n3. Session Context (gaps, state)\n4. Debt (S0/S1, resolution rate)\n5. Learning (effectiveness, automation)\n6. Agent Compliance (code review coverage)\n7. Hook Warnings (7d warnings, false positives)\n8. Skip Abuse (override patterns)\n9. Test Results (pass rate, staleness)\n10. Hook Health (warnings, FP %)\n11. Session State (ongoing gaps)\n12. Pattern Hotspots (violations by type)\n13. Context Usage (memory compaction risk)\n14. Reviews Sync (JSONL staleness)\n15. Review Archive Health (rotation status)\n16. Cross-Document Deps (dependency health)\n\n**Full Mode (+20 categories):** Adds Debt Intake/Resolution, Doc Health, Roadmap, Review Quality, Consolidation, Velocity, Session/Commit Activity, Roadmap Validation/Hygiene, Trigger Compliance, Pattern Sync, Doc Placement, External Links, Unused Deps, Review Churn, Backlog, GitHub Actions, SonarCloud.\n\n**Output Surfaces:**\n- Console: Dashboard with health grade (A-F), score (/100), error/warning/info counts\n- Category Scorecard: Per-category scores & ratings\n- Interactive Walkthrough: Alert-by-alert with Fix Now/Defer/Suppress options\n- Session Log: `.claude/tmp/alert-session-{YYYY-MM-DD-HHMM}.jsonl` (each decision)\n- Suppressions: `.claude/state/alert-suppressions.json` (persistent across sessions)\n\n**State Files:**\n- `.claude/state/alerts-baseline.json` (delta tracking, first run per day)\n- `.claude/tmp/alert-session-*.jsonl` (session decisions, auto-cleaned >7d)\n\n---\n\n## 8. ECOSYSTEM AUDIT SKILLS: Manual Deep Dives\n\n### 8.1 Individual Ecosystem Audits (7 total)\nEach invoked via `npm run` or as part of `/comprehensive-ecosystem-audit` skill.\n\n| Skill | npm Script | Categories | Output | History File |\n|-------|-----------|------------|--------|--------------|\n| TDMS | `npm run tdms:audit` | 12 (debt supply, intake, resolution, metrics, etc.) | Console + findings JSON | `.claude/state/tdms-ecosystem-audit-history.jsonl` |\n| Session | `npm run session:audit` | 10 (gaps, state, activity, logs, etc.) | Console + findings JSON | `.claude/state/session-ecosystem-audit-history.jsonl` |\n| PR Review | `npm run pr:audit` | 18 (skill invocation, pattern enforcement, learning, consolidation, etc.) | Console + findings JSON | `.claude/state/pr-ecosystem-audit.jsonl` |\n| Skills | `npm run skills:audit` | 8 (coverage, config, invocation, compliance) | Console + findings JSON | `.claude/state/skill-ecosystem-audit-history.jsonl` |\n| Docs | `npm run docs:audit` | 9 (staleness, accuracy, cross-refs, placement, external links) | Console + findings JSON | `.claude/state/doc-ecosystem-audit-history.jsonl` |\n| Scripts | `npm run scripts:audit` | 10 (coverage, patterns, testing, consistency) | Console + findings JSON | `.claude/state/script-ecosystem-audit-history.jsonl` |\n| Hooks | `npm run hooks:audit` | 9 (pipeline health, warning lifecycle, false positives, compliance) | Console + findings JSON | `.claude/state/hook-ecosystem-audit-history.jsonl` |\n\n### 8.2 Comprehensive Ecosystem Audit Orchestrator\n**Invocation:** `/comprehensive-ecosystem-audit` skill  \n**Runs:** All 7 audits in staged waves (2-3 audits per wave to manage token budget)  \n**State Management:** `.claude/tmp/comprehensive-ecosystem-audit-progress.json`  \n**Output:** Unified report with all 7 audits + consolidated recommendations\n\n---\n\n## 9. FLAG: NEVER-INVOKED ANALYTICS\n\n| Script/Tool | Reason | Recommendation |\n|-------------|--------|-----------------|\n| `npm run ecosystem:audit:all` | Placeholder in package.json pointing to `/comprehensive-ecosystem-audit` skill | **INTENTIONAL** — force use of skill (not npm run) for wave management |\n| Individual ecosystem audits as `npm run` | Designed to work standalone OR via skill | **OK** — both paths supported |\n| `npm run session:begin` | Not in package.json; uses `/session-begin` skill instead | **INTENTIONAL** — skill provides interactive checklist |\n| `/session-end` | Uses `npm run session:end` internally, not invoked directly | **OK** — wrapper skill manages workflow |\n\n---\n\n## 11. ANALYTICS FLOW DIAGRAM\n\n```\n┌─ Session Start ─────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  1. Dependency hash check                               │\n│  2. Pattern compliance: check-pattern-compliance.js     │\n│  3. Auto-consolidation: run-consolidation.js --auto     │\n│  4. Review sync: reviews:sync --apply                   │\n│  5. Commit log sync: seed-commit-log.js --sync          │\n│  6. Archive rotation (reviews, warnings, health scores) │\n│  7. TDMS health check (S0/S1 counts)                    │\n│  8. Quick health: health/run-health-check.js --quick    │\n│                                                          │\n│  State: .session-state.json, reviews.jsonl,             │\n│         hook-warnings-log.jsonl, health-score-log.jsonl │\n└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n                          ↓\n┌─ Development (Pre-Commit) ──────────────────────────────┐\n│  1. ESLint (BLOCKING)                                   │\n│  2. Tests (CONDITIONAL)                                 │\n│  3. Prettier/lint-staged (AUTO-FIX)                    │\n│  4. Pattern compliance --staged (BLOCKING)              │\n│  5. Audit S0/S1 validation (BLOCKING)                   │\n│  6. CANON schema (WARNING)                              │\n│  7. Requires SKIP_REASON (10-500 chars, single-line, no control chars) for audit trail.\n\n### Finding 2: Hook Warnings Lifecycle\n**Status:** ✓ COMPLETE  \n**Mechanism:** Pre-commit/pre-push append warnings to `.claude/state/hook-warnings-log.jsonl`. Health checker reads, computes false positive %. Alerts skill can suppress or acknowledge. TTL-based cleanup via `cleanup-alert-sessions.js`.\n\n### Finding 3: Pattern Compliance Dual-Gate\n**Status:** ✓ COMPLETE  \n- **Pre-commit:** `--staged` (blocking), checks only changed files\n- **Pre-push:** `push diff only` (warning), re-checks files in push\n- **CI PR:** Changed files (blocking)\n- **CI Push:** All files (non-blocking, weekly full scan)\n\n### Finding 4: Health Score Aggregation\n**Status:** ✓ COMPLETE  \n- **10 individual checkers** (code, security, debt, tests, learning, hooks, session, docs, patterns, ecosystem)\n- **Composite score:** Weighted average (70% core, 8% new state, 9% velocity, 13% full-mode)\n- **Logged to:** health-score-log.jsonl (rotated >30 entries)\n- **Displayed in:** alerts dashboard, session-start quick check\n\n### Finding 5: Session State Tracking\n**Status:** ✓ COMPLETE  \n- `.claude/hooks/.session-state.json` tracks session begin/end times\n- session-start warns if previous session didn't close (>N hours ago)\n- Auto-closes stale sessions to keep counts aligned\n- `/session-end` properly closes with recap\n\n### Finding 6: TDMS Archive Cycle\n**Status:** ✓ COMPLETE  \n- generate-views.js reads from `docs/technical-debt/raw/deduped.jsonl`\n- Scripts appending to MASTER_DEBT.jsonl also append to deduped.jsonl\n- After assign-roadmap-refs.js, copy MASTER_DEBT.jsonl → deduped.jsonl before generate-views.js\n\n### Finding 7: Ecosystem Audit Progress Persistence\n**Status:** ✓ COMPLETE  \n- Each audit skill saves progress to `.claude/tmp/*-progress.json` (<2 hours old resumes)\n- Comprehensive orchestrator manages `.claude/tmp/comprehensive-ecosystem-audit-progress.json`\n- Survives compaction via state file checks on startup\n\n---\n\n## 12. INVOCATION DECISION TREE\n\n**When does what run?**\n\n```\nSession Start (.claude/hooks/session-start.js)\n├─ Always: Dependency check, pattern compliance, review sync, archive rotation\n├─ Conditional: Tests (if config changed)\n└─ Non-blocking: TDMS health, health quick check\n\nPre-Commit (.husky/pre-commit)\n├─ Always: ESLint, Prettier, pattern compliance\n├─ Conditional: Tests (if code changed), audit validation (if audit files)\n├─ Auto-fix: Docs index (regenerates if .md files changed)\n└─ Non-blocking: CANON, skills, agent compliance, hook warnings\n\nPre-Push (.husky/pre-push)\n├─ Always: Circular deps, pattern compliance (push diff)\n└─ Conditional: Code-reviewer coverage check (if scripts changed)\n\nCI on Push/PR (ci.yml)\n├─ Always: Linting, formatting, type check, tests\n├─ On PR: Pattern compliance (changed files)\n├─ On push to main: Pattern compliance all (non-blocking)\n└─ Always: Audit, CANON, TDMS, docs checks\n\nManual Skills\n├─ /session-begin: Interactive startup checklist (calls session:log internally)\n├─ /alerts: Interactive health dashboard (runs health checker + alerts)\n├─ /pr-ecosystem-audit: Deep PR review ecosystem analysis\n├─ /session-ecosystem-audit: Session gaps, state, activity analysis\n├─ /comprehensive-ecosystem-audit: All 7 audits in staged waves\n└─ Individual npm run commands: Direct script execution\n```\n\n---\n\n## 14.
